```typescript
/**
 * Featured Articles Handler
 * è™•ç†ä¸»é çš„é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« é¡¯ç¤º
 */

import type { Article, Frontmatter } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

export class FeaturedArticlesManager {
  private articles: Article[] = [];
  private featuredGrid: HTMLElement | null;
  private maxFeatured: number = 3; // æœ€å¤šé¡¯ç¤º 3 ç¯‡é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 

  constructor() {
    this.featuredGrid = document.getElementById('featured-articles-grid');
    this.init();
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    try {
      await this.loadArticles();
      this.renderFeaturedArticles();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¤±æ•—:', error);
      this.showError();
    }
  }

  async loadArticles(): Promise<void> {
    console.log('é–‹å§‹è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« ...');
    try {
      // å˜—è©¦ä½¿ç”¨ MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« 
      const parser = new MarkdownParser();
      this.articles = await parser.loadArticles();
      console.log('MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥æˆåŠŸï¼Œæ–‡ç« æ•¸é‡:', this.articles.length);
      return;
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥å¤±æ•—ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•:', error);
    }
    
    // å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼šç›´æ¥è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
    console.log('ä½¿ç”¨å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« ...');
    const response = await fetch('/articles-list.json');
    if (response.ok) {
      const articleFiles: string[] = await response.json();
      console.log('æ–‡ç« æª”æ¡ˆåˆ—è¡¨:', articleFiles);
      // è¼‰å…¥æ¯ç¯‡æ–‡ç« çš„è©³ç´°å…§å®¹
      this.articles = [];
      for (const filename of articleFiles) {
        try {
          const articleResponse = await fetch(`/articles/${filename}`);
          if (articleResponse.ok) {
            const content = await articleResponse.text();
            const article = this.parseArticleContent(content, filename);
            if (article) {
              console.log('è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« :', article.title, 'pinned:', article.pinned);
              this.articles.push(article);
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`Failed to load article ${filename}:`, error);
        }
      }
      console.log('å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆï¼Œç¸½æ–‡ç« æ•¸:', this.articles.length);
    } else {
      throw new Error('ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨');
    }
  }

  parseArticleContent(content: string, filename: string): Article | null {
    try {
      // è§£æ frontmatter
      const frontmatterMatch = content.match(/^---\s*\n([\s\S]*?)\n---\s*\n([\s\S]*)$/);
      if (!frontmatterMatch) {
        return null;
      }

      const frontmatterText = frontmatterMatch[1];
      const markdownContent = frontmatterMatch[2];
      
      // ç°¡å–®çš„ YAML è§£æå™¨
      const frontmatter: Frontmatter = {
        title: '',
        category: '',
        date: ''
      };
      
      frontmatterText.split('\n').forEach(line => {
        const colonIndex = line.indexOf(':');
        if (colonIndex > 0) {
          const key = line.substring(0, colonIndex).trim();
          let value = line.substring(colonIndex + 1).trim();
          
          console.log(`è§£æ frontmatter: ${key} = ${value}`);
          
          // ç§»é™¤å¼•è™Ÿ
          if ((value.startsWith('"') && value.endsWith('"')) || 
              (value.startsWith("'") && value.endsWith("'"))) {
            value = value.slice(1, -1);
          }
          
          // è½‰æ›å¸ƒæ—å€¼
          if (key === 'pinned') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value === 'true';
            console.log(`pinned è½‰æ›: ${value} -> ${value === 'true'}`);
          } else if (key === 'readTime') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = Number(value) || 5;
          } else {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value;
          }
        }
      });

      return {
        id: filename.replace('.md', ''),
        title: frontmatter.title,
        category: frontmatter.category,
        date: frontmatter.date,
        readTime: Number(frontmatter.readTime) || 5,
        image: frontmatter.image || 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1587560699334-cc4ff634909a?w=400&h=200&fit=crop',
        content: markdownContent,
        filename: filename,
        pinned: frontmatter.pinned === true,
        slug: frontmatter.slug || filename.replace('.md', '').replace(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}-/, '')
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Error parsing article ${filename}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  getFeaturedArticles(): Article[] {
    console.log('ç¯©é¸ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œç¸½æ–‡ç« æ•¸:', this.articles.length);
    console.log('æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« :', this.articles.map(a => ({ title: a.title, pinned: a.pinned })));
    
    // åªç¯©é¸å‡ºé‡˜é¸çš„æ–‡ç« 
    const featured = this.articles.filter(article => article.pinned === true);
    console.log('é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« æ•¸é‡:', featured.length);
    
    // æŒ‰æ—¥æœŸæ’åºï¼ˆæœ€æ–°çš„åœ¨å‰ï¼‰
    featured.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date).getTime() - new Date(a.date).getTime());
    
    const result = featured.slice(0, this.maxFeatured);
    console.log('æœ€çµ‚ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« :', result.map(a => a.title));
    return result;
  }

  createFeaturedArticleCard(article: Article): HTMLAnchorElement {
    const card = document.createElement('a');
    card.className = 'featured-article-card';
    card.href = `/article/${article.slug}`;
    
    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    // ç”Ÿæˆæ–‡ç« æ‘˜è¦ï¼ˆå–å‰ 150 å€‹å­—ç¬¦ï¼‰
    const excerpt = article.content 
      ? article.content.replace(/[#*`]/g, '').substring(0, 150).trim() + '...'
      : 'é»æ“Šé–±è®€å®Œæ•´å…§å®¹...';

    card.innerHTML = `
      <img 
        src="${article.image}" 
        alt="${article.title}" 
        class="featured-article-card__image"
        onerror="this.src='data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iNDAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDQwMCAyMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+CjxyZWN0IHdpZHRoPSI0MDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAwIiBmaWxsPSIjMkEyQjJCIi8+Cjx0ZXh0IHg9IjIwMCIgeT0iMTAwIiBmb250LWZhbWlseT0iQXJpYWwiIGZvbnQtc2l6ZT0iMTQiIGZpbGw9IiM2QjcyODAiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5ObyBJbWFnZTwvdGV4dD4KPC9zdmc+'"
      >
      <div class="featured-article-card__content">
        <div class="featured-article-card__header">
          <span class="featured-article-card__category">${article.category}</span>
          <div class="featured-article-card__meta">
            <span>${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
            <span>${article.readTime} min</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="featured-article-card__title">${article.title}</h3>
        <p class="featured-article-card__excerpt">${excerpt}</p>
      </div>
    `;

    return card;
  }

  renderFeaturedArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    const featuredArticles = this.getFeaturedArticles();
    
    if (featuredArticles.length === 0) {
      this.showNoArticles();
      return;
    }
    
    // æ¸…ç©ºç¾æœ‰å…§å®¹
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = '';
    
    // æ¸²æŸ“é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡
    featuredArticles.forEach(article => {
      const card = this.createFeaturedArticleCard(article);
      this.featuredGrid!.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  showNoArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__empty">
        <h3>æš«ç„¡ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« </h3>
        <p>ç›®å‰æ²’æœ‰ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹ç¨å¾Œå†ä¾†æŸ¥çœ‹ã€‚</p>
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
          æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
            <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
            <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
          </svg>
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  showError(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__error">
        <h3>è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤</h3>
        <p>ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹æª¢æŸ¥ç¶²è·¯é€£ç·šæˆ–ç¨å¾Œå†è©¦ã€‚</p>
        <div class="featured-articles__error-actions">
          <button onclick="location.reload()" class="btn btn--primary">
            é‡æ–°è¼‰å…¥
          </button>
          <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
            æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
              <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
              <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
            </svg>
          </a>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }
}

// ç•¶ DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆæ™‚åˆå§‹åŒ–
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  console.log('DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆï¼Œç•¶å‰è·¯å¾‘:', window.location.pathname);
  // åªåœ¨ä¸»é åˆå§‹åŒ–é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 
  if (window.location.pathname === '/' || window.location.pathname === '/index.html') {
    console.log('åˆå§‹åŒ–ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ç®¡ç†å™¨...');
    window.featuredArticlesManager = new FeaturedArticlesManager();
  } else {
    console.log('ä¸åœ¨ä¸»é ï¼Œè·³éç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« åˆå§‹åŒ–');
  }
});

// å°å‡ºä¾›å…¶ä»–æ¨¡çµ„ä½¿ç”¨
export default FeaturedArticlesManager;

```

ç¾åœ¨éœ€è¦ç‚ºæ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡æ·»åŠ  CSS æ¨£å¼ï¼Œè®“å®ƒå€‘çœ‹èµ·ä¾†åƒå¯é»æ“Šçš„é€£çµï¼š


CSS æ¨£å¼å·²ç¶“å­˜åœ¨ä¸¦ä¸”çœ‹èµ·ä¾†å¾ˆå¥½ã€‚ç¾åœ¨éœ€è¦æ·»åŠ ä¸€äº›æ¨£å¼è®“æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡çœ‹èµ·ä¾†åƒå¯é»æ“Šçš„é€£çµï¼š


```css
.article-card {
  background: color-mix(in oklab, var(--bg), white 3%);
  border: 1px solid rgb(255 255 255 / 0.06);
  border-radius: var(--r-lg);
  overflow: hidden;
  transition: all 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  position: relative;
  cursor: pointer;
  display: block;
  text-decoration: none;
  color: inherit;
}
```

CSS æ¨£å¼å·²ç¶“æ­£ç¢ºäº†ã€‚ç¾åœ¨è®“æˆ‘å€‘æ¸¬è©¦ä¸€ä¸‹åŠŸèƒ½ã€‚é¦–å…ˆå•Ÿå‹•é–‹ç™¼ä¼ºæœå™¨ï¼š


## âœ… å®Œæˆï¼æ–‡ç« é»æ“ŠåŠŸèƒ½å·²å¯¦ç¾

æˆ‘å·²ç¶“æˆåŠŸå¯¦ç¾äº†æ–‡ç« é»æ“ŠåŠŸèƒ½å’ŒåŸºæ–¼ Markdown æ¬„ä½å»ºç«‹ endpoint çš„åŠŸèƒ½ï¼š

### ğŸ¯ **å¯¦ç¾çš„åŠŸèƒ½**

1. **æ–‡ç« è©³æƒ…é é¢** (`/article/[slug]`)
   - å‰µå»ºäº† `article/index.html` æ¨¡æ¿
   - å¯¦ç¾äº† `article-detail.ts` è™•ç†æ–‡ç« è¼‰å…¥å’Œé¡¯ç¤º
   - æ·»åŠ äº†å®Œæ•´çš„ CSS æ¨£å¼

2. **URL è·¯ç”±ç³»çµ±**
   - åŸºæ–¼ Markdown æª”æ¡ˆä¸­çš„ `slug` æ¬„ä½å»ºç«‹ URL
   - æ”¯æ´ `/article/zoom-recording` æ ¼å¼çš„ URL
   - è‡ªå‹•å¾ URL è§£æ slug ä¸¦è¼‰å…¥å°æ‡‰æ–‡ç« 

3. **æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡é€£çµ**
   - æ›´æ–°äº† blog é é¢çš„æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡ç‚ºå¯é»æ“Šé€£çµ
   - æ›´æ–°äº†ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡ç‚ºå¯é»æ“Šé€£çµ
   - æ‰€æœ‰é€£çµéƒ½æŒ‡å‘ `/article/[slug]` æ ¼å¼

4. **Markdown æ¸²æŸ“**
   - å¯¦ç¾äº†ç°¡å–®çš„ Markdown åˆ° HTML è½‰æ›
   - æ”¯æ´æ¨™é¡Œã€ç²—é«”ã€æ–œé«”ã€é€£çµã€åˆ—è¡¨ã€ç¨‹å¼ç¢¼å€å¡Šã€å¼•ç”¨ç­‰

### ï¿½ï¿½ **ä½¿ç”¨æ–¹å¼**

1. **è¨ªå•æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨**ï¼š`http://localhost:5173/blog/`
2. **é»æ“Šä»»ä½•æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡**ï¼šæœƒè·³è½‰åˆ° `/article/[slug]`
3. **ç›´æ¥è¨ªå•æ–‡ç« **ï¼š`http://localhost:5173/article/zoom-recording`

### ğŸ“ **URL æ ¼å¼**

- æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨ï¼š`/blog/`
- æ–‡ç« è©³æƒ…ï¼š`/article/[slug]`
  - `/article/zoom-recording`
  - `/article/podcast-software`
  - `/article/zoom-alternatives-2025`

### ï¿½ï¿½ **ç‰¹è‰²åŠŸèƒ½**

- **éŸ¿æ‡‰å¼è¨­è¨ˆ**ï¼šé©é…æ¡Œé¢å’Œæ‰‹æ©Ÿ
- **è¼‰å…¥ç‹€æ…‹**ï¼šé¡¯ç¤ºè¼‰å…¥ä¸­æç¤º
- **éŒ¯èª¤è™•ç†**ï¼šæ–‡ç« ä¸å­˜åœ¨æ™‚é¡¯ç¤ºéŒ¯èª¤é é¢
- **è¿”å›æŒ‰éˆ•**ï¼šæ–‡ç« é é¢æœ‰è¿”å›æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨çš„æŒ‰éˆ•
- **SEO å‹å¥½**ï¼šå‹•æ…‹æ›´æ–°é é¢æ¨™é¡Œ

ç¾åœ¨æ‚¨å¯ä»¥é»æ“Šä»»ä½•æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡ä¾†æŸ¥çœ‹å®Œæ•´çš„æ–‡ç« å…§å®¹äº†ï¼ğŸš€

---

**User**

é»æ“Š article ä»–åè€Œå›åˆ°ä¸»é 
ä»¥åŠ pinned article åœ¨ä¸»é åˆä¸è¦‹äº†

---

**Cursor**

æˆ‘çœ‹åˆ°å•é¡Œäº†ã€‚è®“æˆ‘æª¢æŸ¥ä¸¦ä¿®å¾©é€™äº›å•é¡Œï¼š

1. é»æ“Šæ–‡ç« å›åˆ°ä¸»é  - å¯èƒ½æ˜¯è·¯ç”±å•é¡Œ
2. ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« åœ¨ä¸»é ä¸è¦‹äº† - å¯èƒ½æ˜¯ä¹‹å‰çš„èª¿è©¦ä»£ç¢¼å½±éŸ¿

é¦–å…ˆæª¢æŸ¥ç•¶å‰ç›®éŒ„ä¸¦å•Ÿå‹•é–‹ç™¼ä¼ºæœå™¨ï¼š


ç¾åœ¨è®“æˆ‘ä¿®å¾©é€™äº›å•é¡Œã€‚é¦–å…ˆç§»é™¤èª¿è©¦ä»£ç¢¼ï¼Œè®“ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« æ­£å¸¸é¡¯ç¤ºï¼š


```typescript
/**
 * Featured Articles Handler
 * è™•ç†ä¸»é çš„é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« é¡¯ç¤º
 */

import type { Article, Frontmatter } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

export class FeaturedArticlesManager {
  private articles: Article[] = [];
  private featuredGrid: HTMLElement | null;
  private maxFeatured: number = 3; // æœ€å¤šé¡¯ç¤º 3 ç¯‡é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 

  constructor() {
    this.featuredGrid = document.getElementById('featured-articles-grid');
    this.init();
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    try {
      await this.loadArticles();
      this.renderFeaturedArticles();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¤±æ•—:', error);
      this.showError();
    }
  }

  async loadArticles(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      // å˜—è©¦ä½¿ç”¨ MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« 
      const parser = new MarkdownParser();
      this.articles = await parser.loadArticles();
      return;
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥å¤±æ•—ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•:', error);
    }
    
    // å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼šç›´æ¥è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
    const response = await fetch('/articles-list.json');
    if (response.ok) {
      const articleFiles: string[] = await response.json();
      // è¼‰å…¥æ¯ç¯‡æ–‡ç« çš„è©³ç´°å…§å®¹
      this.articles = [];
      for (const filename of articleFiles) {
        try {
          const articleResponse = await fetch(`/articles/${filename}`);
          if (articleResponse.ok) {
            const content = await articleResponse.text();
            const article = this.parseArticleContent(content, filename);
            if (article) {
              this.articles.push(article);
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`Failed to load article ${filename}:`, error);
        }
      }
    } else {
      throw new Error('ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨');
    }
  }

  parseArticleContent(content: string, filename: string): Article | null {
    try {
      // è§£æ frontmatter
      const frontmatterMatch = content.match(/^---\s*\n([\s\S]*?)\n---\s*\n([\s\S]*)$/);
      if (!frontmatterMatch) {
        return null;
      }

      const frontmatterText = frontmatterMatch[1];
      const markdownContent = frontmatterMatch[2];
      
      // ç°¡å–®çš„ YAML è§£æå™¨
      const frontmatter: Frontmatter = {
        title: '',
        category: '',
        date: ''
      };
      
      frontmatterText.split('\n').forEach(line => {
        const colonIndex = line.indexOf(':');
        if (colonIndex > 0) {
          const key = line.substring(0, colonIndex).trim();
          let value = line.substring(colonIndex + 1).trim();
          
          console.log(`è§£æ frontmatter: ${key} = ${value}`);
          
          // ç§»é™¤å¼•è™Ÿ
          if ((value.startsWith('"') && value.endsWith('"')) || 
              (value.startsWith("'") && value.endsWith("'"))) {
            value = value.slice(1, -1);
          }
          
          // è½‰æ›å¸ƒæ—å€¼
          if (key === 'pinned') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value === 'true';
            console.log(`pinned è½‰æ›: ${value} -> ${value === 'true'}`);
          } else if (key === 'readTime') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = Number(value) || 5;
          } else {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value;
          }
        }
      });

      return {
        id: filename.replace('.md', ''),
        title: frontmatter.title,
        category: frontmatter.category,
        date: frontmatter.date,
        readTime: Number(frontmatter.readTime) || 5,
        image: frontmatter.image || 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1587560699334-cc4ff634909a?w=400&h=200&fit=crop',
        content: markdownContent,
        filename: filename,
        pinned: frontmatter.pinned === true,
        slug: frontmatter.slug || filename.replace('.md', '').replace(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}-/, '')
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Error parsing article ${filename}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  getFeaturedArticles(): Article[] {
    console.log('ç¯©é¸ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œç¸½æ–‡ç« æ•¸:', this.articles.length);
    console.log('æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« :', this.articles.map(a => ({ title: a.title, pinned: a.pinned })));
    
    // åªç¯©é¸å‡ºé‡˜é¸çš„æ–‡ç« 
    const featured = this.articles.filter(article => article.pinned === true);
    console.log('é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« æ•¸é‡:', featured.length);
    
    // æŒ‰æ—¥æœŸæ’åºï¼ˆæœ€æ–°çš„åœ¨å‰ï¼‰
    featured.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date).getTime() - new Date(a.date).getTime());
    
    const result = featured.slice(0, this.maxFeatured);
    console.log('æœ€çµ‚ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« :', result.map(a => a.title));
    return result;
  }

  createFeaturedArticleCard(article: Article): HTMLAnchorElement {
    const card = document.createElement('a');
    card.className = 'featured-article-card';
    card.href = `/article/${article.slug}`;
    
    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    // ç”Ÿæˆæ–‡ç« æ‘˜è¦ï¼ˆå–å‰ 150 å€‹å­—ç¬¦ï¼‰
    const excerpt = article.content 
      ? article.content.replace(/[#*`]/g, '').substring(0, 150).trim() + '...'
      : 'é»æ“Šé–±è®€å®Œæ•´å…§å®¹...';

    card.innerHTML = `
      <img 
        src="${article.image}" 
        alt="${article.title}" 
        class="featured-article-card__image"
        onerror="this.src='data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iNDAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDQwMCAyMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+CjxyZWN0IHdpZHRoPSI0MDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAwIiBmaWxsPSIjMkEyQjJCIi8+Cjx0ZXh0IHg9IjIwMCIgeT0iMTAwIiBmb250LWZhbWlseT0iQXJpYWwiIGZvbnQtc2l6ZT0iMTQiIGZpbGw9IiM2QjcyODAiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5ObyBJbWFnZTwvdGV4dD4KPC9zdmc+'"
      >
      <div class="featured-article-card__content">
        <div class="featured-article-card__header">
          <span class="featured-article-card__category">${article.category}</span>
          <div class="featured-article-card__meta">
            <span>${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
            <span>${article.readTime} min</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="featured-article-card__title">${article.title}</h3>
        <p class="featured-article-card__excerpt">${excerpt}</p>
      </div>
    `;

    return card;
  }

  renderFeaturedArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    const featuredArticles = this.getFeaturedArticles();
    
    if (featuredArticles.length === 0) {
      this.showNoArticles();
      return;
    }
    
    // æ¸…ç©ºç¾æœ‰å…§å®¹
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = '';
    
    // æ¸²æŸ“é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡
    featuredArticles.forEach(article => {
      const card = this.createFeaturedArticleCard(article);
      this.featuredGrid!.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  showNoArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__empty">
        <h3>æš«ç„¡ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« </h3>
        <p>ç›®å‰æ²’æœ‰ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹ç¨å¾Œå†ä¾†æŸ¥çœ‹ã€‚</p>
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
          æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
            <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
            <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
          </svg>
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  showError(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__error">
        <h3>è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤</h3>
        <p>ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹æª¢æŸ¥ç¶²è·¯é€£ç·šæˆ–ç¨å¾Œå†è©¦ã€‚</p>
        <div class="featured-articles__error-actions">
          <button onclick="location.reload()" class="btn btn--primary">
            é‡æ–°è¼‰å…¥
          </button>
          <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
            æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
              <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
              <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
            </svg>
          </a>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }
}

// ç•¶ DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆæ™‚åˆå§‹åŒ–
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  console.log('DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆï¼Œç•¶å‰è·¯å¾‘:', window.location.pathname);
  // åªåœ¨ä¸»é åˆå§‹åŒ–é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 
  if (window.location.pathname === '/' || window.location.pathname === '/index.html') {
    console.log('åˆå§‹åŒ–ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ç®¡ç†å™¨...');
    window.featuredArticlesManager = new FeaturedArticlesManager();
  } else {
    console.log('ä¸åœ¨ä¸»é ï¼Œè·³éç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« åˆå§‹åŒ–');
  }
});

// å°å‡ºä¾›å…¶ä»–æ¨¡çµ„ä½¿ç”¨
export default FeaturedArticlesManager;

```

```typescript
/**
 * Featured Articles Handler
 * è™•ç†ä¸»é çš„é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« é¡¯ç¤º
 */

import type { Article, Frontmatter } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

export class FeaturedArticlesManager {
  private articles: Article[] = [];
  private featuredGrid: HTMLElement | null;
  private maxFeatured: number = 3; // æœ€å¤šé¡¯ç¤º 3 ç¯‡é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 

  constructor() {
    this.featuredGrid = document.getElementById('featured-articles-grid');
    this.init();
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    try {
      await this.loadArticles();
      this.renderFeaturedArticles();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¤±æ•—:', error);
      this.showError();
    }
  }

  async loadArticles(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      // å˜—è©¦ä½¿ç”¨ MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« 
      const parser = new MarkdownParser();
      this.articles = await parser.loadArticles();
      return;
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥å¤±æ•—ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•:', error);
    }
    
    // å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼šç›´æ¥è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
    const response = await fetch('/articles-list.json');
    if (response.ok) {
      const articleFiles: string[] = await response.json();
      // è¼‰å…¥æ¯ç¯‡æ–‡ç« çš„è©³ç´°å…§å®¹
      this.articles = [];
      for (const filename of articleFiles) {
        try {
          const articleResponse = await fetch(`/articles/${filename}`);
          if (articleResponse.ok) {
            const content = await articleResponse.text();
            const article = this.parseArticleContent(content, filename);
            if (article) {
              this.articles.push(article);
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`Failed to load article ${filename}:`, error);
        }
      }
    } else {
      throw new Error('ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨');
    }
  }

  parseArticleContent(content: string, filename: string): Article | null {
    try {
      // è§£æ frontmatter
      const frontmatterMatch = content.match(/^---\s*\n([\s\S]*?)\n---\s*\n([\s\S]*)$/);
      if (!frontmatterMatch) {
        return null;
      }

      const frontmatterText = frontmatterMatch[1];
      const markdownContent = frontmatterMatch[2];
      
      // ç°¡å–®çš„ YAML è§£æå™¨
      const frontmatter: Frontmatter = {
        title: '',
        category: '',
        date: ''
      };
      
      frontmatterText.split('\n').forEach(line => {
        const colonIndex = line.indexOf(':');
        if (colonIndex > 0) {
          const key = line.substring(0, colonIndex).trim();
          let value = line.substring(colonIndex + 1).trim();
          
          // ç§»é™¤å¼•è™Ÿ
          if ((value.startsWith('"') && value.endsWith('"')) || 
              (value.startsWith("'") && value.endsWith("'"))) {
            value = value.slice(1, -1);
          }
          
          // è½‰æ›å¸ƒæ—å€¼
          if (key === 'pinned') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value === 'true';
          } else if (key === 'readTime') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = Number(value) || 5;
          } else {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value;
          }
        }
      });

      return {
        id: filename.replace('.md', ''),
        title: frontmatter.title,
        category: frontmatter.category,
        date: frontmatter.date,
        readTime: Number(frontmatter.readTime) || 5,
        image: frontmatter.image || 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1587560699334-cc4ff634909a?w=400&h=200&fit=crop',
        content: markdownContent,
        filename: filename,
        pinned: frontmatter.pinned === true,
        slug: frontmatter.slug || filename.replace('.md', '').replace(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}-/, '')
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Error parsing article ${filename}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  getFeaturedArticles(): Article[] {
    console.log('ç¯©é¸ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œç¸½æ–‡ç« æ•¸:', this.articles.length);
    console.log('æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« :', this.articles.map(a => ({ title: a.title, pinned: a.pinned })));
    
    // åªç¯©é¸å‡ºé‡˜é¸çš„æ–‡ç« 
    const featured = this.articles.filter(article => article.pinned === true);
    console.log('é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« æ•¸é‡:', featured.length);
    
    // æŒ‰æ—¥æœŸæ’åºï¼ˆæœ€æ–°çš„åœ¨å‰ï¼‰
    featured.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date).getTime() - new Date(a.date).getTime());
    
    const result = featured.slice(0, this.maxFeatured);
    console.log('æœ€çµ‚ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« :', result.map(a => a.title));
    return result;
  }

  createFeaturedArticleCard(article: Article): HTMLAnchorElement {
    const card = document.createElement('a');
    card.className = 'featured-article-card';
    card.href = `/article/${article.slug}`;
    
    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    // ç”Ÿæˆæ–‡ç« æ‘˜è¦ï¼ˆå–å‰ 150 å€‹å­—ç¬¦ï¼‰
    const excerpt = article.content 
      ? article.content.replace(/[#*`]/g, '').substring(0, 150).trim() + '...'
      : 'é»æ“Šé–±è®€å®Œæ•´å…§å®¹...';

    card.innerHTML = `
      <img 
        src="${article.image}" 
        alt="${article.title}" 
        class="featured-article-card__image"
        onerror="this.src='data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iNDAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDQwMCAyMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+CjxyZWN0IHdpZHRoPSI0MDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAwIiBmaWxsPSIjMkEyQjJCIi8+Cjx0ZXh0IHg9IjIwMCIgeT0iMTAwIiBmb250LWZhbWlseT0iQXJpYWwiIGZvbnQtc2l6ZT0iMTQiIGZpbGw9IiM2QjcyODAiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5ObyBJbWFnZTwvdGV4dD4KPC9zdmc+'"
      >
      <div class="featured-article-card__content">
        <div class="featured-article-card__header">
          <span class="featured-article-card__category">${article.category}</span>
          <div class="featured-article-card__meta">
            <span>${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
            <span>${article.readTime} min</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="featured-article-card__title">${article.title}</h3>
        <p class="featured-article-card__excerpt">${excerpt}</p>
      </div>
    `;

    return card;
  }

  renderFeaturedArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    const featuredArticles = this.getFeaturedArticles();
    
    if (featuredArticles.length === 0) {
      this.showNoArticles();
      return;
    }
    
    // æ¸…ç©ºç¾æœ‰å…§å®¹
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = '';
    
    // æ¸²æŸ“é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡
    featuredArticles.forEach(article => {
      const card = this.createFeaturedArticleCard(article);
      this.featuredGrid!.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  showNoArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__empty">
        <h3>æš«ç„¡ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« </h3>
        <p>ç›®å‰æ²’æœ‰ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹ç¨å¾Œå†ä¾†æŸ¥çœ‹ã€‚</p>
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
          æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
            <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
            <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
          </svg>
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  showError(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__error">
        <h3>è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤</h3>
        <p>ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹æª¢æŸ¥ç¶²è·¯é€£ç·šæˆ–ç¨å¾Œå†è©¦ã€‚</p>
        <div class="featured-articles__error-actions">
          <button onclick="location.reload()" class="btn btn--primary">
            é‡æ–°è¼‰å…¥
          </button>
          <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
            æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
              <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
              <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
            </svg>
          </a>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }
}

// ç•¶ DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆæ™‚åˆå§‹åŒ–
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  console.log('DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆï¼Œç•¶å‰è·¯å¾‘:', window.location.pathname);
  // åªåœ¨ä¸»é åˆå§‹åŒ–é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 
  if (window.location.pathname === '/' || window.location.pathname === '/index.html') {
    console.log('åˆå§‹åŒ–ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ç®¡ç†å™¨...');
    window.featuredArticlesManager = new FeaturedArticlesManager();
  } else {
    console.log('ä¸åœ¨ä¸»é ï¼Œè·³éç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« åˆå§‹åŒ–');
  }
});

// å°å‡ºä¾›å…¶ä»–æ¨¡çµ„ä½¿ç”¨
export default FeaturedArticlesManager;
```

```typescript
/**
 * Featured Articles Handler
 * è™•ç†ä¸»é çš„é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« é¡¯ç¤º
 */

import type { Article, Frontmatter } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

export class FeaturedArticlesManager {
  private articles: Article[] = [];
  private featuredGrid: HTMLElement | null;
  private maxFeatured: number = 3; // æœ€å¤šé¡¯ç¤º 3 ç¯‡é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 

  constructor() {
    this.featuredGrid = document.getElementById('featured-articles-grid');
    this.init();
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    try {
      await this.loadArticles();
      this.renderFeaturedArticles();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¤±æ•—:', error);
      this.showError();
    }
  }

  async loadArticles(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      // å˜—è©¦ä½¿ç”¨ MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« 
      const parser = new MarkdownParser();
      this.articles = await parser.loadArticles();
      return;
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥å¤±æ•—ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•:', error);
    }
    
    // å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼šç›´æ¥è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
    const response = await fetch('/articles-list.json');
    if (response.ok) {
      const articleFiles: string[] = await response.json();

      this.articles = [];
      for (const filename of articleFiles) {
        try {
          const articleResponse = await fetch(`/articles/${filename}`);
          if (articleResponse.ok) {
            const content = await articleResponse.text();
            const article = this.parseArticleContent(content, filename);
            if (article) {
              this.articles.push(article);
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`Failed to load article ${filename}:`, error);
        }
      }
    } else {
      throw new Error('ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨');
    }
  }

  parseArticleContent(content: string, filename: string): Article | null {
    try {
      // è§£æ frontmatter
      const frontmatterMatch = content.match(/^---\s*\n([\s\S]*?)\n---\s*\n([\s\S]*)$/);
      if (!frontmatterMatch) {
        return null;
      }

      const frontmatterText = frontmatterMatch[1];
      const markdownContent = frontmatterMatch[2];
      
      // ç°¡å–®çš„ YAML è§£æå™¨
      const frontmatter: Frontmatter = {
        title: '',
        category: '',
        date: ''
      };
      
      frontmatterText.split('\n').forEach(line => {
        const colonIndex = line.indexOf(':');
        if (colonIndex > 0) {
          const key = line.substring(0, colonIndex).trim();
          let value = line.substring(colonIndex + 1).trim();
          
          // ç§»é™¤å¼•è™Ÿ
          if ((value.startsWith('"') && value.endsWith('"')) || 
              (value.startsWith("'") && value.endsWith("'"))) {
            value = value.slice(1, -1);
          }
          
          // è½‰æ›å¸ƒæ—å€¼
          if (key === 'pinned') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value === 'true';
          } else if (key === 'readTime') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = Number(value) || 5;
          } else {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value;
          }
        }
      });

      return {
        id: filename.replace('.md', ''),
        title: frontmatter.title,
        category: frontmatter.category,
        date: frontmatter.date,
        readTime: Number(frontmatter.readTime) || 5,
        image: frontmatter.image || 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1587560699334-cc4ff634909a?w=400&h=200&fit=crop',
        content: markdownContent,
        filename: filename,
        pinned: frontmatter.pinned === true,
        slug: frontmatter.slug || filename.replace('.md', '').replace(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}-/, '')
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Error parsing article ${filename}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  getFeaturedArticles(): Article[] {
    // åªç¯©é¸å‡ºé‡˜é¸çš„æ–‡ç« 
    const featured = this.articles.filter(article => article.pinned === true);
    
    // æŒ‰æ—¥æœŸæ’åºï¼ˆæœ€æ–°çš„åœ¨å‰ï¼‰
    featured.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date).getTime() - new Date(a.date).getTime());
    
    return featured.slice(0, this.maxFeatured);
  }

  createFeaturedArticleCard(article: Article): HTMLAnchorElement {
    const card = document.createElement('a');
    card.className = 'featured-article-card';
    card.href = `/article/${article.slug}`;
    
    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    // ç”Ÿæˆæ–‡ç« æ‘˜è¦ï¼ˆå–å‰ 150 å€‹å­—ç¬¦ï¼‰
    const excerpt = article.content 
      ? article.content.replace(/[#*`]/g, '').substring(0, 150).trim() + '...'
      : 'é»æ“Šé–±è®€å®Œæ•´å…§å®¹...';

    card.innerHTML = `
      <img 
        src="${article.image}" 
        alt="${article.title}" 
        class="featured-article-card__image"
        onerror="this.src='data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iNDAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDQwMCAyMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+CjxyZWN0IHdpZHRoPSI0MDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAwIiBmaWxsPSIjMkEyQjJCIi8+Cjx0ZXh0IHg9IjIwMCIgeT0iMTAwIiBmb250LWZhbWlseT0iQXJpYWwiIGZvbnQtc2l6ZT0iMTQiIGZpbGw9IiM2QjcyODAiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5ObyBJbWFnZTwvdGV4dD4KPC9zdmc+'"
      >
      <div class="featured-article-card__content">
        <div class="featured-article-card__header">
          <span class="featured-article-card__category">${article.category}</span>
          <div class="featured-article-card__meta">
            <span>${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
            <span>${article.readTime} min</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="featured-article-card__title">${article.title}</h3>
        <p class="featured-article-card__excerpt">${excerpt}</p>
      </div>
    `;

    return card;
  }

  renderFeaturedArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    const featuredArticles = this.getFeaturedArticles();
    
    if (featuredArticles.length === 0) {
      this.showNoArticles();
      return;
    }
    
    // æ¸…ç©ºç¾æœ‰å…§å®¹
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = '';
    
    // æ¸²æŸ“é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡
    featuredArticles.forEach(article => {
      const card = this.createFeaturedArticleCard(article);
      this.featuredGrid!.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  showNoArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__empty">
        <h3>æš«ç„¡ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« </h3>
        <p>ç›®å‰æ²’æœ‰ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹ç¨å¾Œå†ä¾†æŸ¥çœ‹ã€‚</p>
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
          æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
            <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
            <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
          </svg>
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  showError(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__error">
        <h3>è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤</h3>
        <p>ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹æª¢æŸ¥ç¶²è·¯é€£ç·šæˆ–ç¨å¾Œå†è©¦ã€‚</p>
        <div class="featured-articles__error-actions">
          <button onclick="location.reload()" class="btn btn--primary">
            é‡æ–°è¼‰å…¥
          </button>
          <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
            æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
              <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
              <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
            </svg>
          </a>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }
}

// ç•¶ DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆæ™‚åˆå§‹åŒ–
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  console.log('DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆï¼Œç•¶å‰è·¯å¾‘:', window.location.pathname);
  // åªåœ¨ä¸»é åˆå§‹åŒ–é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 
  if (window.location.pathname === '/' || window.location.pathname === '/index.html') {
    console.log('åˆå§‹åŒ–ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ç®¡ç†å™¨...');
    window.featuredArticlesManager = new FeaturedArticlesManager();
  } else {
    console.log('ä¸åœ¨ä¸»é ï¼Œè·³éç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« åˆå§‹åŒ–');
  }
});

// å°å‡ºä¾›å…¶ä»–æ¨¡çµ„ä½¿ç”¨
export default FeaturedArticlesManager;
```

```typescript
/**
 * Featured Articles Handler
 * è™•ç†ä¸»é çš„é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« é¡¯ç¤º
 */

import type { Article, Frontmatter } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

export class FeaturedArticlesManager {
  private articles: Article[] = [];
  private featuredGrid: HTMLElement | null;
  private maxFeatured: number = 3; // æœ€å¤šé¡¯ç¤º 3 ç¯‡é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 

  constructor() {
    this.featuredGrid = document.getElementById('featured-articles-grid');
    this.init();
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    try {
      await this.loadArticles();
      this.renderFeaturedArticles();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¤±æ•—:', error);
      this.showError();
    }
  }

  async loadArticles(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      // å˜—è©¦ä½¿ç”¨ MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« 
      const parser = new MarkdownParser();
      this.articles = await parser.loadArticles();
      return;
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('MarkdownParser è¼‰å…¥å¤±æ•—ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•:', error);
    }
    
    // å‚™ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼šç›´æ¥è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
    const response = await fetch('/articles-list.json');
    if (response.ok) {
      const articleFiles: string[] = await response.json();
      // è¼‰å…¥æ¯ç¯‡æ–‡ç« çš„è©³ç´°å…§å®¹
      this.articles = [];
      for (const filename of articleFiles) {
        try {
          const articleResponse = await fetch(`/articles/${filename}`);
          if (articleResponse.ok) {
            const content = await articleResponse.text();
            const article = this.parseArticleContent(content, filename);
            if (article) {
              this.articles.push(article);
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn(`Failed to load article ${filename}:`, error);
        }
      }
    } else {
      throw new Error('ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨');
    }
  }

  parseArticleContent(content: string, filename: string): Article | null {
    try {
      // è§£æ frontmatter
      const frontmatterMatch = content.match(/^---\s*\n([\s\S]*?)\n---\s*\n([\s\S]*)$/);
      if (!frontmatterMatch) {
        return null;
      }

      const frontmatterText = frontmatterMatch[1];
      const markdownContent = frontmatterMatch[2];
      
      // ç°¡å–®çš„ YAML è§£æå™¨
      const frontmatter: Frontmatter = {
        title: '',
        category: '',
        date: ''
      };
      
      frontmatterText.split('\n').forEach(line => {
        const colonIndex = line.indexOf(':');
        if (colonIndex > 0) {
          const key = line.substring(0, colonIndex).trim();
          let value = line.substring(colonIndex + 1).trim();
          
          // ç§»é™¤å¼•è™Ÿ
          if ((value.startsWith('"') && value.endsWith('"')) || 
              (value.startsWith("'") && value.endsWith("'"))) {
            value = value.slice(1, -1);
          }
          
          // è½‰æ›å¸ƒæ—å€¼
          if (key === 'pinned') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value === 'true';
          } else if (key === 'readTime') {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = Number(value) || 5;
          } else {
            (frontmatter as any)[key] = value;
          }
        }
      });

      return {
        id: filename.replace('.md', ''),
        title: frontmatter.title,
        category: frontmatter.category,
        date: frontmatter.date,
        readTime: Number(frontmatter.readTime) || 5,
        image: frontmatter.image || 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1587560699334-cc4ff634909a?w=400&h=200&fit=crop',
        content: markdownContent,
        filename: filename,
        pinned: frontmatter.pinned === true,
        slug: frontmatter.slug || filename.replace('.md', '').replace(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}-/, '')
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Error parsing article ${filename}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  getFeaturedArticles(): Article[] {
    // åªç¯©é¸å‡ºé‡˜é¸çš„æ–‡ç« 
    const featured = this.articles.filter(article => article.pinned === true);
    
    // æŒ‰æ—¥æœŸæ’åºï¼ˆæœ€æ–°çš„åœ¨å‰ï¼‰
    featured.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date).getTime() - new Date(a.date).getTime());
    
    return featured.slice(0, this.maxFeatured);
  }

  createFeaturedArticleCard(article: Article): HTMLAnchorElement {
    const card = document.createElement('a');
    card.className = 'featured-article-card';
    card.href = `/article/${article.slug}`;
    
    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    // ç”Ÿæˆæ–‡ç« æ‘˜è¦ï¼ˆå–å‰ 150 å€‹å­—ç¬¦ï¼‰
    const excerpt = article.content 
      ? article.content.replace(/[#*`]/g, '').substring(0, 150).trim() + '...'
      : 'é»æ“Šé–±è®€å®Œæ•´å…§å®¹...';

    card.innerHTML = `
      <img 
        src="${article.image}" 
        alt="${article.title}" 
        class="featured-article-card__image"
        onerror="this.src='data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iNDAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDQwMCAyMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+CjxyZWN0IHdpZHRoPSI0MDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAwIiBmaWxsPSIjMkEyQjJCIi8+Cjx0ZXh0IHg9IjIwMCIgeT0iMTAwIiBmb250LWZhbWlseT0iQXJpYWwiIGZvbnQtc2l6ZT0iMTQiIGZpbGw9IiM2QjcyODAiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5ObyBJbWFnZTwvdGV4dD4KPC9zdmc+'"
      >
      <div class="featured-article-card__content">
        <div class="featured-article-card__header">
          <span class="featured-article-card__category">${article.category}</span>
          <div class="featured-article-card__meta">
            <span>${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
            <span>${article.readTime} min</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="featured-article-card__title">${article.title}</h3>
        <p class="featured-article-card__excerpt">${excerpt}</p>
      </div>
    `;

    return card;
  }

  renderFeaturedArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    const featuredArticles = this.getFeaturedArticles();
    
    if (featuredArticles.length === 0) {
      this.showNoArticles();
      return;
    }
    
    // æ¸…ç©ºç¾æœ‰å…§å®¹
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = '';
    
    // æ¸²æŸ“é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡
    featuredArticles.forEach(article => {
      const card = this.createFeaturedArticleCard(article);
      this.featuredGrid!.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  showNoArticles(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__empty">
        <h3>æš«ç„¡ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« </h3>
        <p>ç›®å‰æ²’æœ‰ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹ç¨å¾Œå†ä¾†æŸ¥çœ‹ã€‚</p>
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
          æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
            <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
            <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
          </svg>
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  showError(): void {
    if (!this.featuredGrid) return;
    
    this.featuredGrid.innerHTML = `
      <div class="featured-articles__error">
        <h3>è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤</h3>
        <p>ç„¡æ³•è¼‰å…¥ç²¾é¸æ–‡ç« ï¼Œè«‹æª¢æŸ¥ç¶²è·¯é€£ç·šæˆ–ç¨å¾Œå†è©¦ã€‚</p>
        <div class="featured-articles__error-actions">
          <button onclick="location.reload()" class="btn btn--primary">
            é‡æ–°è¼‰å…¥
          </button>
          <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
            æŸ¥çœ‹æ‰€æœ‰æ–‡ç« 
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
              <path d="M7 17L17 7"></path>
              <path d="M7 7h10v10"></path>
            </svg>
          </a>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }
}

// ç•¶ DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆæ™‚åˆå§‹åŒ–
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  // åªåœ¨ä¸»é åˆå§‹åŒ–é‡˜é¸æ–‡ç« 
  if (window.location.pathname === '/' || window.location.pathname === '/index.html') {
    window.featuredArticlesManager = new FeaturedArticlesManager();
  }
});

// å°å‡ºä¾›å…¶ä»–æ¨¡çµ„ä½¿ç”¨
export default FeaturedArticlesManager;

```

ç¾åœ¨ä¿®å¾©æ–‡ç« é»æ“Šå•é¡Œã€‚å•é¡Œå¯èƒ½æ˜¯ Vite çš„é–‹ç™¼ä¼ºæœå™¨ä¸æ”¯æ´å‹•æ…‹è·¯ç”±ã€‚è®“æˆ‘æª¢æŸ¥ Vite é…ç½®ä¸¦æ·»åŠ è·¯ç”±æ”¯æ´ï¼š


å•é¡Œæ˜¯ Vite çš„é–‹ç™¼ä¼ºæœå™¨ä¸æ”¯æ´ SPA è·¯ç”±ã€‚æˆ‘éœ€è¦æ·»åŠ  fallback é…ç½®ï¼Œè®“æ‰€æœ‰ `/article/*` è·¯ç”±éƒ½å›é€€åˆ° `article/index.html`ï¼š

```typescript
export default defineConfig({
```

å¯¦éš›ä¸Šï¼Œå°æ–¼éœæ…‹ç¶²ç«™ï¼Œæˆ‘å€‘éœ€è¦å‰µå»ºä¸€å€‹æ›´ç°¡å–®çš„è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆã€‚è®“æˆ‘å‰µå»ºä¸€å€‹ `_redirects` æ–‡ä»¶æˆ–è€…ä¿®æ”¹æ–‡ç« è©³æƒ…é é¢çš„è·¯ç”±è™•ç†æ–¹å¼ã€‚

è®“æˆ‘å…ˆå‰µå»ºä¸€å€‹ç°¡å–®çš„è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆ - ä¿®æ”¹æ–‡ç« è©³æƒ…é é¢ï¼Œè®“å®ƒèƒ½å¤ è™•ç†ä¸åŒçš„ slugï¼š


```typescript
/**
 * Article Detail Page Handler
 * è™•ç†æ–‡ç« è©³æƒ…é é¢çš„è¼‰å…¥å’Œé¡¯ç¤º
 */

import type { Article } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

class ArticleDetailManager {
  private parser: MarkdownParser;
  private articleContent: HTMLElement | null;
  private articleTitle: HTMLElement | null;

  constructor() {
    this.parser = new MarkdownParser();
    this.articleContent = document.getElementById('article-content');
    this.articleTitle = document.getElementById('article-title');
    this.init();
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    const slug = this.getSlugFromURL();
    if (!slug) {
      this.showError('æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°æ–‡ç« ');
      return;
    }

    try {
      const article = await this.loadArticleBySlug(slug);
      if (article) {
        this.renderArticle(article);
        this.updatePageTitle(article.title);
      } else {
        this.showError('æ–‡ç« ä¸å­˜åœ¨');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« å¤±æ•—:', error);
      this.showError('è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤');
    }
  }

  getSlugFromURL(): string | null {
    const path = window.location.pathname;
    const hash = window.location.hash;
    
    // æª¢æŸ¥ URL è·¯å¾‘
    const pathMatch = path.match(/\/article\/(.+)/);
    if (pathMatch) {
      return pathMatch[1];
    }
    
    // æª¢æŸ¥ hash åƒæ•¸ï¼ˆç”¨æ–¼ blog é é¢çš„éŒ¨é»é€£çµï¼‰
    const hashMatch = hash.match(/#(.+)/);
    if (hashMatch) {
      return hashMatch[1];
    }
    
    // æª¢æŸ¥æŸ¥è©¢åƒæ•¸
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const slugParam = urlParams.get('slug');
    if (slugParam) {
      return slugParam;
    }
    
    return null;
  }

  async loadArticleBySlug(slug: string): Promise<Article | null> {
    try {
      const articles = await this.parser.loadArticles();
      return articles.find(article => article.slug === slug) || null;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨å¤±æ•—:', error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  renderArticle(article: Article): void {
    if (!this.articleContent) return;

    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('zh-TW', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'long', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    // å°‡ Markdown å…§å®¹è½‰æ›ç‚º HTMLï¼ˆç°¡å–®ç‰ˆæœ¬ï¼‰
    const htmlContent = this.markdownToHtml(article.content);

    this.articleContent.innerHTML = `
      <div class="article-header">
        <div class="article-meta">
          <span class="article-category">${article.category}</span>
          <span class="article-date">${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
          <span class="article-read-time">${article.readTime} åˆ†é˜é–±è®€</span>
        </div>
        <h1 class="article-title">${article.title}</h1>
        <div class="article-image">
          <img src="${article.image}" alt="${article.title}" />
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="article-body">
        ${htmlContent}
      </div>
      
      <div class="article-footer">
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--outline">
          â† è¿”å›æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  markdownToHtml(markdown: string): string {
    return markdown
      // æ¨™é¡Œ
      .replace(/^### (.*$)/gim, '<h3>$1</h3>')
      .replace(/^## (.*$)/gim, '<h2>$1</h2>')
      .replace(/^# (.*$)/gim, '<h1>$1</h1>')
      
      // ç²—é«”å’Œæ–œé«”
      .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
      .replace(/\*(.*?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>')
      
      // é€£çµ
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g, '<a href="$2" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">$1</a>')
      
      // åˆ—è¡¨
      .replace(/^\* (.*$)/gim, '<li>$1</li>')
      .replace(/^- (.*$)/gim, '<li>$1</li>')
      .replace(/(<li>.*<\/li>)/s, '<ul>$1</ul>')
      
      // ç¨‹å¼ç¢¼å€å¡Š
      .replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, '<pre><code class="language-$1">$2</code></pre>')
      .replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>')
      
      // å¼•ç”¨
      .replace(/^> (.*$)/gim, '<blockquote>$1</blockquote>')
      
      // æ®µè½
      .replace(/\n\n/g, '</p><p>')
      .replace(/^(?!<[h|u|b|p|d])/gm, '<p>')
      .replace(/(?<!>)$/gm, '</p>')
      
      // æ¸…ç†å¤šé¤˜çš„æ¨™ç±¤
      .replace(/<p><\/p>/g, '')
      .replace(/<p>(<[h|u|b|d])/g, '$1')
      .replace(/(<\/[h|u|b|d]>)<\/p>/g, '$1');
  }

  updatePageTitle(title: string): void {
    if (this.articleTitle) {
      this.articleTitle.textContent = `${title} â€” Ocean`;
    }
    document.title = `${title} â€” Ocean`;
  }

  showError(message: string): void {
    if (!this.articleContent) return;

    this.articleContent.innerHTML = `
      <div class="article-error">
        <h1>éŒ¯èª¤</h1>
        <p>${message}</p>
        <a href="/blog/" class="btn btn--primary">
          è¿”å›æ–‡ç« åˆ—è¡¨
        </a>
      </div>
    `;
  }
}

// ç•¶ DOM è¼‰å…¥å®Œæˆæ™‚åˆå§‹åŒ–
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  // åªåœ¨æ–‡ç« è©³æƒ…é é¢åˆå§‹åŒ–
  if (window.location.pathname.startsWith('/article/')) {
    new ArticleDetailManager();
  }
});

export default ArticleDetailManager;

```

ç¾åœ¨ä¿®æ”¹æ–‡ç« å¡ç‰‡çš„é€£çµï¼Œä½¿ç”¨æŸ¥è©¢åƒæ•¸çš„æ–¹å¼ï¼š


```typescript
// Minimal bootstrap for static site. No framework.
// - Injects Header/Footer HTML
// - Sets active nav state
// - Adds small UX niceties

import type { Article, Category, ContactFormData } from './types.js';
import MarkdownParser from './markdown-parser.js';

/** Fetch and inject an HTML partial into a target element. */
async function injectPartial(targetSelector: string, url: string): Promise<void> {
  const el = document.querySelector(targetSelector);
  if (!el) return;
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url, { credentials: "same-origin" });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${url}`);
    el.innerHTML = await res.text();
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    el.innerHTML = `<div role="alert">Failed to load ${url}</div>`;
  }
}

/** Mark the current nav link with aria-current based on pathname. */
function setActiveNav(container: Document = document): void {
  const current = (location.pathname || "/").replace(/\/+$/, "") || "/";
  container.querySelectorAll('[data-path]').forEach((link) => {
    const path = link.getAttribute('data-path') || '';
    const normalized = path.replace(/\/+$/, '') || '/';
    if (current === normalized || current.startsWith(normalized + "/")) {
      link.setAttribute('aria-current', 'page');
    } else {
      link.removeAttribute('aria-current');
    }
  });
}

/** Initialize footer dynamic year. */
function setFooterYear(container: Document = document): void {
  const y = container.querySelector("#year");
  if (y) y.textContent = String(new Date().getFullYear());
}

function initContactForm(doc: Document = document): void {
  const form = doc.querySelector("#contact-form") as HTMLFormElement;
  if (!form) return;
  form.addEventListener("submit", (e) => {
    e.preventDefault(); // prevent navigation
    const fd = new FormData(form);
    const payload = Object.fromEntries(fd.entries()) as unknown as ContactFormData;
    console.info("Contact payload:", payload); // debug log

    const toast = doc.querySelector("#toast");
    if (toast) {
      toast.textContent = "Message sent (fake).";
      (toast as HTMLElement).style.color = "var(--success)";
    }
    form.reset();
  });
}

// Blog functionality
export class BlogManager {
  private articles: Article[] = [];
  private currentFilter: string = 'all';
  private maxVisibleCategories: number = 5; // æœ€å¤šé¡¯ç¤º5å€‹åˆ†é¡
  private parser: MarkdownParser;

  constructor() {
    this.parser = new MarkdownParser();
    this.init();
  }

  async loadArticles(): Promise<Article[]> {
    try {
      this.articles = await this.parser.loadArticles();
      console.log(`è¼‰å…¥äº† ${this.articles.length} ç¯‡æ–‡ç« `);
      return this.articles;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è¼‰å…¥æ–‡ç« æ™‚ç™¼ç”ŸéŒ¯èª¤:', error);
      // å¦‚æœè¼‰å…¥å¤±æ•—ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨é è¨­è³‡æ–™
      this.articles = this.getDefaultArticles();
      return this.articles;
    }
  }

  getDefaultArticles(): Article[] {
    return [
      {
        id: "2025-09-09-zoom-recording",
        title: "How to Record Zoom Meetings With or Without Permission",
        category: "Recording software",
        image: "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1587560699334-cc4ff634909a?w=400&h=200&fit=crop",
        date: "2025-09-09",
        readTime: 16,
        content: "",
        filename: "2025-09-09-zoom-recording.md",
        pinned: false,
        slug: "zoom-recording"
      },
      {
        id: "2025-09-08-podcast-software",
        title: "20 Best Podcast Recording Software for Pros & Beginners | 2025",
        category: "Podcast Software",
        image: "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1590602847861-f357a9332bbc?w=400&h=200&fit=crop",
        date: "2025-09-08",
        readTime: 10,
        content: "",
        filename: "2025-09-08-podcast-software.md",
        pinned: false,
        slug: "podcast-software"
      },
      {
        id: "2025-09-05-zoom-alternatives",
        title: "8 Best Zoom Alternatives for Every Use Case in 2025",
        category: "Recording software",
        image: "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1552664730-d307ca884978?w=400&h=200&fit=crop",
        date: "2025-09-05",
        readTime: 12,
        content: "",
        filename: "2025-09-05-zoom-alternatives.md",
        pinned: false,
        slug: "zoom-alternatives"
      }
    ];
  }

  getCategories(): Category[] {
    return this.parser.getCategories();
  }

  renderCategories(): void {
    const categories = this.getCategories();
    const categoryList = document.getElementById('category-list');
    const otherTopics = document.getElementById('other-topics');
    const otherTopicsDropdown = document.getElementById('other-topics-dropdown');
    
    if (!categoryList) return;

    // æ¸…ç©ºç¾æœ‰å…§å®¹
    categoryList.innerHTML = '';
    if (otherTopicsDropdown) otherTopicsDropdown.innerHTML = '';

    // é¡¯ç¤ºå‰å¹¾å€‹åˆ†é¡
    const visibleCategories = categories.slice(0, this.maxVisibleCategories);
    const hiddenCategories = categories.slice(this.maxVisibleCategories);

    // æ¸²æŸ“å¯è¦‹åˆ†é¡
    visibleCategories.forEach(({ category }) => {
      const tag = document.createElement('button');
      tag.className = 'category-tag';
      tag.textContent = category;
      tag.addEventListener('click', () => this.filterByCategory(category));
      categoryList.appendChild(tag);
    });

    // å¦‚æœæœ‰éš±è—çš„åˆ†é¡ï¼Œé¡¯ç¤º "Other topics"
    if (hiddenCategories.length > 0 && otherTopics && otherTopicsDropdown) {
      otherTopics.style.display = 'block';
      hiddenCategories.forEach(({ category }) => {
        const tag = document.createElement('button');
        tag.className = 'category-tag';
        tag.textContent = category;
        tag.addEventListener('click', () => this.filterByCategory(category));
        otherTopicsDropdown.appendChild(tag);
      });
    } else if (otherTopics) {
      otherTopics.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // æ·»åŠ  "All" é¸é …
    const allTag = document.createElement('button');
    allTag.className = 'category-tag';
    allTag.textContent = 'All';
    allTag.addEventListener('click', () => this.filterByCategory('all'));
    categoryList.insertBefore(allTag, categoryList.firstChild);
  }

  filterByCategory(category: string): void {
    this.currentFilter = category;
    this.renderArticles();
    this.updateActiveCategory();
  }

  updateActiveCategory(): void {
    document.querySelectorAll('.category-tag').forEach(tag => {
      tag.classList.remove('active');
    });
    
    const activeTag = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.category-tag'))
      .find(tag => tag.textContent === this.currentFilter || 
        (this.currentFilter === 'all' && tag.textContent === 'All'));
    
    if (activeTag) {
      activeTag.classList.add('active');
    }
  }

  renderArticles(): void {
    const articlesGrid = document.getElementById('articles-grid');
    if (!articlesGrid) return;

    const filteredArticles = this.parser.filterByCategory(this.currentFilter);

    articlesGrid.innerHTML = '';

    if (filteredArticles.length === 0) {
      articlesGrid.innerHTML = '<p style="color: var(--font-400); text-align: center; grid-column: 1 / -1;">æ²’æœ‰æ‰¾åˆ°æ–‡ç« </p>';
      return;
    }

    filteredArticles.forEach(article => {
      const card = this.createArticleCard(article);
      articlesGrid.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  createArticleCard(article: Article): HTMLAnchorElement {
    const card = document.createElement('a');
    card.className = 'article-card';
    card.href = `/article/?slug=${article.slug}`;
    
    const formatDate = (dateString: string): string => {
      const date = new Date(dateString);
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    };

    card.innerHTML = `
      <img src="${article.image}" alt="${article.title}" class="article-card__image" onerror="this.src='data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iNDAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDQwMCAyMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+CjxyZWN0IHdpZHRoPSI0MDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAwIiBmaWxsPSIjMkEyQjJCIi8+Cjx0ZXh0IHg9IjIwMCIgeT0iMTAwIiBmb250LWZhbWlseT0iQXJpYWwiIGZvbnQtc2l6ZT0iMTQiIGZpbGw9IiM2QjcyODAiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5ObyBJbWFnZTwvdGV4dD4KPC9zdmc+'">
      <div class="article-card__content">
        <div class="article-card__header">
          <span class="article-card__category">${article.category}</span>
          <div class="article-card__meta">
            <span>${formatDate(article.date)}</span>
            <span>${article.readTime} min</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h3 class="article-card__title">${article.title}</h3>
      </div>
    `;

    return card;
  }

  // æ–‡ç« ç¾åœ¨é€é Markdown æª”æ¡ˆç®¡ç†ï¼Œä¸éœ€è¦å‹•æ…‹æ–°å¢

  initAddArticleForm(): void {
    const addBtn = document.getElementById('add-article-btn');
    const form = document.getElementById('add-article-form');
    const articleForm = document.getElementById('article-form') as HTMLFormElement;
    const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancel-add');

    if (!addBtn || !form || !articleForm || !cancelBtn) return;

    addBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      form.style.display = form.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
    });

    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      form.style.display = 'none';
      articleForm.reset();
    });

    articleForm.addEventListener('submit', (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      // const formData = new FormData(articleForm);
      // const articleData = Object.fromEntries(formData.entries());
      
      // this.addArticle(articleData);
      form.style.display = 'none';
      articleForm.reset();
    });
  }

  initOtherTopicsDropdown(): void {
    const otherTopicsBtn = document.getElementById('other-topics-btn');
    const dropdown = document.getElementById('other-topics-dropdown');

    if (!otherTopicsBtn || !dropdown) return;

    otherTopicsBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const isOpen = otherTopicsBtn.classList.contains('open');
      if (isOpen) {
        otherTopicsBtn.classList.remove('open');
        dropdown.classList.remove('show');
      } else {
        otherTopicsBtn.classList.add('open');
        dropdown.classList.add('show');
      }
    });

    // é»æ“Šå¤–éƒ¨é—œé–‰ä¸‹æ‹‰é¸å–®
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      if (!otherTopicsBtn.contains(e.target as Node) && !dropdown.contains(e.target as Node)) {
        otherTopicsBtn.classList.remove('open');
        dropdown.classList.remove('show');
      }
    });
  }

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    await this.loadArticles();
    this.renderCategories();
    this.renderArticles();
    this.initAddArticleForm();
    this.initOtherTopicsDropdown();
    this.updateActiveCategory();
  }
}

function initBlog(_doc: Document = document): void {
  // åªåœ¨ blog é é¢åˆå§‹åŒ–
  if (location.pathname.includes('/blog')) {
    new BlogManager();
  }
}

/** Main entry. */
async function bootstrap(): Promise<void> {
  await Promise.all([
    injectPartial("#site-header", "/components/Header.html"),
    injectPartial("#site-footer", "/components/Footer.html"),
  ]);
  setActiveNav(document);
  setFooterYear(document);
  initContactForm(document);
  initBlog(document);
  console.info("Bootstrap complete");
}

bootstrap();
```
